cron.ParseStandard(schedule); err != nil {\n                allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(fldPath, schedule, err.Error()))\n        }\n        switch {\n        case allowTZInSchedule && strings.Contains(schedule, \"TZ\") && timeZone != nil:\n                allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(fldPath, schedule, \"cannot use both timeZone field and TZ or CRON_TZ in schedule\"))\n        case !allowTZInSchedule && strings.Contains(schedule, \"TZ\"):\n                allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(fldPath, schedule, \"cannot use TZ or CRON_TZ in schedule, use timeZone not use the file name components '.' and '..'.\n// * Within a file name component, use only ASCII letters, '.', '-' and '_'.\n// * Do not use digits, as that might create an ambiguity with POSIX TZ strings.\n// * A file name component must not exceed 14 characters or start with '-'\n//\n// 0-9 and + characters are tolerated to accommodate legacy compatibility names\nvar validTimeZoneCharacters = regexp.MustCompile(`^[A-Za-z\\.\\-_0-9+]{1,14}$`)\n\nfunc validateTimeZone(timeZone *string, fldPath *field.Path) field.ErrorList {\n        allErrs := field.ErrorList{}\n        if timeZone == nil {\n                return allErrs\n        }\n\n        if len(*timeZone) == 0 {\n                allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(fldPath, timeZone, \"timeZone must be nil or non-empty string\"))\n                return allErrs\n        }\n\n        for _, part := range strings.Split(*timeZone, \"/\") {\n                if part == \".\" || part == \"..\" || strings.HasPrefix(part, \"-\") || !validTimeZoneCharacters.MatchString(part) {\n                        allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(fldPath, timeZone, fmt.Sprintf(\"unknown time zone %s\", *timeZone)))\n                        return allErrs\n                }\n        }\n\n        if strings.EqualFold(*timeZone, \"Local\") {\n                allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(fldPath, timeZone, \"timeZone must be an explicit time zone as defined in https://www.iana.org/time-zones\"))\n        }\n\n        if _, err := time.LoadLocation(*timeZone); err != nil {\n                allErrs = append(allErrs, field.Invalid(fldPath, timeZone, err.Error()))\n        }\n\n        return allErrs\n}\n\n// ValidateJobTemplateSpec validates a JobTemplateSpec and returns an ErrorList with any copied via `unsafe.Pointer` in all generated conversion functions; validated only on change during updates (compatibility accommodation); deliberately omitted from the fuzzer to avoid round-trip test failures on random strings.\n\n4. **Validation Changes** \u2014 `ValidateCronJobCreate` enforces the 52-character name limit (63 \u2212 11 suffix chars); The difference is purely stylistic: v1 uses `ptr.To(false)` / `ptr.To[int32](3)` (modern `k8s.io/utils/ptr`); v1beta1 uses `new(bool)` / `new(int32)` + dereference-assign (older Go idiom, never updated because v1beta1 was already deprecated). v1 additionally defines `SetDefaults_Job` (full Job spec defaulting); v1beta1 has no Job defaulting at all.\n\n6. **Bonus \u2014 GC Policy Divergence** \u2014 The single behavioral difference between versions at runtime: `strategy.DefaultGarbageCollectionPolicy` returns `OrphanDependents` for `batch/v1beta1` requests and `DeleteDependents` for all others, preserving the original 1.8 garbage collection semantics for legacy clients while correcting it for GA users.\n\n7. **Complete Conversion Chain Trace** \u2014 Step-by-step trace for both a v1beta1 GET and a v1 create, showing exactly which generated functions are called and in what order."
